                  <h4>
                   <a href="/press/final-tally-travel-lost-11-trillion-us-economic-output-20">
                    Final Tally: Travel Lost $1.1 Trillion in U.S. Economic Output in ‘20
                   </a>
                  </h4>
                  <em>
                   <span class="date-display-single" content="2021-03-17T00:00:00-04:00" datatype="xsd:dateTime" property="dc:date">
                    March 17, 2021
                   </span>
                  </em>
                  <p>
                   Travel’s economic footprint in the United States shrank a staggering 42% last year, from $2.6 trillion to $1.5 trillion, according to new
                   <a href="https://www.ustravel.org/system/files/media_root/document/Research_Fact-Sheet_Industry-Table.pdf\">
                    end-of-year totals
                   </a>
                   prepared for the U.S. Travel Association by the research firm Tourism Economics.
                  </p>
                  <strong class="read-more-link bright-red sans">
                   <a href="/press/final-tally-travel-lost-11-trillion-us-economic-output-20">
                    Read More
                   </a>
                  </strong>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="views-slideshow-cycle-main-frame-row-item views-row views-row-0 views-row-odd medium-4 small-12 columns">

                   <img alt="Policy: Image of the Capitol, Washington, DC" src="https://www.ustravel.org/sites/default/files/styles/320_x_180/public/media_root/image/Policy-2.jpg?itok=7J5hP0Lh" title="Policy: Image of the Capitol, Washington, DC" typeof="foaf:Image"/>

                  </h4>
                  <em>
                   <span class="date-display-single" content="2021-03-12T00:00:00-05:00" datatype="xsd:dateTime" property="dc:date">
                    March 12, 2021
                   </span>
                  </em>
                  <p>
                   The U.S. Travel Association on Friday voiced strong support for the
                   <a href="https://www.shaheen.senate.gov/news/press/shaheen-collins-cardin-introduce-bill-to-extend-ppp">
                    PPP Extension Act of 2021
                   </a>
                   , a
                   <a href="https://luetkemeyer.house.gov/news/documentsingle.aspx?DocumentID=400492">
                    bipartisan
                   </a>
                   and
                   <a href="https://www.shaheen.senate.gov/news/press/shaheen-collins-cardin-introduce-bill-to-extend-ppp">
                    bicameral
                   </a>
                   bill.
                  </p>
                  <strong class="read-more-link bright-red sans">
                   <a href="/press/us-travel-endorses-ppp-extension-bill-urges-swift-passage">
                    Read More
                   </a>
                  </strong>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>

                  <h4>
                   <a href="/news/us-travel-applauds-covid-relief-package">
                    U.S. Travel Applauds COVID Relief Package
                   </a>
                  </h4>
                  <em>
                   <span class="date-display-single" content="2021-03-12T00:00:00-05:00" datatype="xsd:dateTime" property="dc:date">
                    March 12, 2021
                   </span>
                  </em>
                  <p>
                   President Biden signed the
                   <a href="https://www.congress.gov/bill/117th-congress/house-bill/1319/text">
                    American Rescue Plan Act of 2021
                   </a>
                   into law.
                  </p>

               <h4>
                <a href="/research/fact-sheet-travel-creates-jobs">
                 Fact Sheet: Travel Creates Jobs
                </a>
               </h4>
               <div>
                Travel is essential to the American economy, providing an indispensable source of job creation. The travel industry is unique: it is highly dependent on human labor, generally immune to outsourcing and plays a key role in international trade.
               </div>
               <div>

                </a>
